<h1 class="gb-headline gb-headline-03b77ca2 gb-headline-text">Welcome to Invent Your Recipe!</h1>



<div class="wp-block-group"><div class="wp-block-group__inner-container is-layout-constrained wp-block-group-is-layout-constrained">
<p class="has-var-contrast-color has-text-color" style="font-size:22px">Hi, I&rsquo;m Tom, a Maryland-based food blogger, recipe developer, and cookbook author, and whether you&rsquo;re a beginner, an experienced home cook, or somewhere in between, you&rsquo;ve found the right place.</p>



<p class="has-var-contrast-color has-text-color" style="font-size:22px">Here, I focus on simple, everyday dishes that you can easily customize with different ingredients. I provide base recipes along with alternative ingredient suggestions. My commitment is real food and no AI images!</p>



<p class="has-var-contrast-color has-text-color" style="font-size:22px">My unique approach? I cook without recipes, then write down what I did! It&rsquo;s my style, and I hope you find it inspiring.</p>



<p class="has-var-contrast-color has-text-color" style="font-size:22px">Interested in seeing how I cook? Grab your <strong><a href="https://milotree.com/freebie/1518" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">free eCookbook</a></strong>! I also hope you&rsquo;ll join the conversation in the comments section of my recipes.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div>
</div>



<div style="height:40px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>



<div style="height:40px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">My Commitment: Real Food Recipes And No AI Images</h3>



<p>In a world where the internet is increasingly filled with AI-generated content, I want to be clear about the blueprint of this blog. </p>



<p>At Invent Your Recipe, I am committed to real food and real photography.</p>



<p>I&rsquo;ve always been analytical in nature, and to me, a recipe is an invention that requires a human touch. </p>



<p>You cannot &ldquo;cook by feel&rdquo; with an image created by a machine. You can&rsquo;t hear the sizzle of the pan or smell the garlic saut&eacute;ing through an algorithm.</p>



<p>My process relies on the tactile, the weight of the skillet, the sound of the knife on the board, and the trial-and-error of testing a dish before it makes the &ldquo;starting lineup.&rdquo;</p>



<p>When you see a photo here, it&rsquo;s a photograph of a meal I actually made in my kitchen. </p>



<p>When you read a recipe, you can trust it&rsquo;s a reliable <strong><a href="https://inventyourrecipe.com/how-to-invent-a-recipe/" data-type="page" data-id="22312">base recipe</a></strong> that has been systematically tested for clarity and repeatability.</p>



<p>I&rsquo;m a busy Dad who cooks for my family 6-7 nights a week; I know you don&rsquo;t have time for a &ldquo;machine generated&rdquo; ingredient list that doesn&rsquo;t work. </p>



<p>You&rsquo;re here for honest, simple, and delicious food that you can reproduce in your own home without the overwhelm.</p>



<p>Everything here is human-created and human-photographed. No shortcuts, just the same hard work and sacrifice my family brought with them in the 1960s. </p>



<p>Because at the end of the day, you can&rsquo;t feed your soul with a digital imitation.</p>



<div style="height:20px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>

<div class="wp-block-group"><div class="wp-block-group__inner-container is-layout-constrained wp-block-group-is-layout-constrained">
<div style="height:20px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>



<h3 class="gb-headline gb-headline-fd27f6fa gb-headline-text"><strong>The Concept of Invent Your Recipe</strong></h3>



<p>The idea for this website came about from me trying to write down recipes for my wife, who wanted to be able to cook the dishes I love. </p>



<p>As I began writing recipes down I found it difficult because I always change the ways I prepare dishes, I like to create, not emulate. </p>



<p>The name &ldquo;Invent Your Recipe&rdquo; was a direct result of the idea of creating.</p>



<p>And the motto for this idea of Invent Your Recipe is: Create, Taste, Innovate</p>



<p>I hope that this website can serve as a platform for&nbsp;<a href="https://inventyourrecipe.com/contact-us/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"><strong>sharing ideas</strong></a>&nbsp;and for pushing the boundaries of contemporary dishes. </p>



<p>To learn more about me, check out the <strong><a href="https://inventyourrecipe.com/about/" data-type="page" data-id="2127" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">about the cook</a></strong> page, and I look forward to inventing recipes with you!</p>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-uagb-container uagb-block-cm9pbyrk alignfull uagb-is-root-container"><div class="uagb-container-inner-blocks-wrap">
<div class="wp-block-uagb-image alignleft uagb-block-fnro4bau wp-block-uagb-image--layout-default wp-block-uagb-image--effect-static wp-block-uagb-image--align-left"><figure class="wp-block-uagb-image__figure"><a class="" href="https://inventyourrecipe.com/how-to-invent-a-recipe/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"><img decoding="async" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;%20width=&#039;564&#039;%20height=&#039;423&#039;%20viewBox=&#039;0%200%20564%20423&#039;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="How To Create Home-Made Recipes" class="uag-image-22350 perfmatters-lazy" width="564" height="423" title="How To Create Home-Made Recipes" role="img" data-pin-title="How To Create Home-Made Recipes" data-pin-description="How To Create Home-Made Recipes" data-src="https://inventyourrecipe.com/wp-content/uploads/How-To-Invent-A-Recipe-Post6.webp" data-srcset="https://inventyourrecipe.com/wp-content/uploads/How-To-Invent-A-Recipe-Post6.webp ,https://inventyourrecipe.com/wp-content/uploads/How-To-Invent-A-Recipe-Post6.webp 780w, https://inventyourrecipe.com/wp-content/uploads/How-To-Invent-A-Recipe-Post6.webp 360w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 480px) 150px" /></a></figure></div>

<div class="wp-block-uagb-info-box uagb-block-wr6qsenh uagb-infobox__content-wrap  uagb-infobox-icon-left uagb-infobox-left uagb-infobox-image-valign-top"><div class="uagb-ifb-icon-wrap"><div class="uagb-iconbox-icon-wrap uagb-infobox-shape-circle"><svg xmlns="https://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewbox="0 0 448 512"><path d="M438.6 105.4C451.1 117.9 451.1 138.1 438.6 150.6L182.6 406.6C170.1 419.1 149.9 419.1 137.4 406.6L9.372 278.6C-3.124 266.1-3.124 245.9 9.372 233.4C21.87 220.9 42.13 220.9 54.63 233.4L159.1 338.7L393.4 105.4C405.9 92.88 426.1 92.88 438.6 105.4H438.6z"></path></svg></div></div><div class="uagb-ifb-content"><div class="uagb-ifb-title-wrap"><h4 class="uagb-ifb-title">Invent or Create?</h4></div><p class="uagb-ifb-desc">I am analytical and technical in nature, so I invent my recipes, but you can use whichever word you like. After all, it is about enjoying the process and making yourself some great tasting food, without being overwhelmed.<br></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-uagb-info-box uagb-block-g9y2dsxk uagb-infobox__content-wrap  uagb-infobox-icon-left uagb-infobox-left uagb-infobox-image-valign-top"><div class="uagb-ifb-icon-wrap"><div class="uagb-iconbox-icon-wrap uagb-infobox-shape-circle"><svg xmlns="https://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewbox="0 0 448 512"><path d="M438.6 105.4C451.1 117.9 451.1 138.1 438.6 150.6L182.6 406.6C170.1 419.1 149.9 419.1 137.4 406.6L9.372 278.6C-3.124 266.1-3.124 245.9 9.372 233.4C21.87 220.9 42.13 220.9 54.63 233.4L159.1 338.7L393.4 105.4C405.9 92.88 426.1 92.88 438.6 105.4H438.6z"></path></svg></div></div><div class="uagb-ifb-content"><div class="uagb-ifb-title-wrap"><h4 class="uagb-ifb-title">Embrace Your Style, But Try New Things</h4></div><p class="uagb-ifb-desc">Lean into what you like to cook and how you like to cook it. Make it your default cooking style. But also see the benefit and value in trying new things.&nbsp;<br></p></div></div>
</div>
</div></div>



<div style="height:20px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>



<div class="wp-block-group"><div class="wp-block-group__inner-container is-layout-constrained wp-block-group-is-layout-constrained">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Create Your Own Recipes</strong></h3>



<p>Are you interested in creating your own recipes? I hope so because cooking, creating, and eating is a lot of fun! </p>



<p>Especially when you get friends and family to contribute to the cooking and eating experience.</p>



<p>Creating lifelong memories is an important part of cooking for me. Spending time with loved ones in the kitchen is my happy place.</p>



<p>Looking for a framework or guide for creating recipes? I have just the thing. Check out this page, <strong><a href="https://inventyourrecipe.com/how-to-invent-a-recipe/" target="_blank" data-type="page" data-id="22312" rel="noreferrer noopener">How to Invent A Recipe</a></strong>, to get started.</p>



<p>Included are an introduction to my &ldquo;base recipe&rdquo; concept, steps to invent a recipe, and tips for creating your starting lineup of base recipes.</p>
</div></div>



<div style="height:20px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>

<h2 class="gb-headline gb-headline-1095594c gb-headline-text"><strong>Fan Favorite Recipes</strong></h2>


<div class="gb-grid-wrapper gb-grid-wrapper-dd96d78d gb-query-loop-wrapper">
<div class="gb-grid-column gb-grid-column-bdedb94b gb-query-loop-item post-11175 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-vegetarian category-side-dish tag-cabbage tag-cruciferous-vegetables tag-featured tag-garlic tag-green-beans tag-healthy tag-onions tag-stir-fry tag-tomatoes tag-vegetarian grow-content-main grow-content-body"><div class="gb-container gb-container-bdedb94b">
<figure class="gb-block-image gb-block-image-0d722db2"><img decoding="async" width="600" height="800" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;%20width=&#039;600&#039;%20height=&#039;800&#039;%20viewBox=&#039;0%200%20600%20800&#039;%3E%3C/svg%3E" class="gb-image-0d722db2 perfmatters-lazy" alt="Stir Fry Cabbage with Green Beans: Feature Image" title="Invent Your Recipe 5" data-src="https://inventyourrecipe.com/wp-content/uploads/Stir-Fry-Cabbage-with-Green-Beans_Feature-Image.webp" data-srcset="https://inventyourrecipe.com/wp-content/uploads/Stir-Fry-Cabbage-with-Green-Beans_Feature-Image.webp 600w, https://inventyourrecipe.com/wp-content/uploads/Stir-Fry-Cabbage-with-Green-Beans_Feature-Image-150x200.webp 150w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px" /></figure>

<h2 class="gb-headline gb-headline-b96d9746 gb-headline-text"><strong>Chicken Recipes</strong></h2>

<div class="gb-headline gb-headline-32a93df8 gb-headline-text">There&rsquo;s something about pasta meals without meat that just hits the spot: simple ingredients, bold flavors, and nothing too heavy.</div>
</div></div>
</div>
